## Idea

A type is
{{#concept "finite" Disambiguation="type" Agda=is-finite WD="finite set" WDID=Q272404}}
if it is [merely equivalent](foundation.mere-equivalences.md) to a
[standard finite type](univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.md).

**Terminology.** This finiteness condition is also referred to as _Bishop
finiteness_. (Cf. the external links at the bottom of this page)

## Definition

### The type of all finite types of a universe level

<pre class="Agda"><a id="𝔽ᵉ"></a><a id="2731" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2731" class="Function">𝔽ᵉ</a> <a id="2734" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2736" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2737" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2737" class="Bound">lᵉ</a> <a id="2740" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2742" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="2747" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2749" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2751" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="2755" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2756" href="Agda.Primitive.html#931" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="2761" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2737" class="Bound">lᵉ</a><a id="2763" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Types with finite cardinality `k`

## Properties

### Finite types are closed under equivalences

<pre class="Agda"><a id="4322" class="Keyword">abstract</a>
  <a id="is-finite-equivᵉ"></a><a id="4333" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4333" class="Function">is-finite-equivᵉ</a> <a id="4350" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="4356" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4357" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4357" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="4361" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4361" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="4365" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4367" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4372" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4374" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4375" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4375" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="4378" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4380" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="4384" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4357" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a><a id="4387" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4389" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4390" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4390" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="4393" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4395" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="4399" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4361" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="4402" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4404" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4405" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4405" class="Bound">eᵉ</a> <a id="4408" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4410" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4375" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="4413" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2662" class="Function Operator">≃ᵉ</a> <a id="4416" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4390" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a><a id="4418" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4420" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="4426" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2285" class="Function">is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="4437" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4375" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="4440" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4442" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2285" class="Function">is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="4453" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4390" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a>
  <a id="4458" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4333" class="Function">is-finite-equivᵉ</a> <a id="4475" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4475" class="Bound">eᵉ</a> <a id="4478" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="4484" href="foundation.propositional-truncations%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5725" class="Function">map-universal-property-trunc-Propᵉ</a>

  <a id="6489" href="foundation.propositional-truncations%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1593" class="Function">unit-trunc-Propᵉ</a> <a id="6506" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6507" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1298" class="Function">equiv-countᵉ</a> <a id="6520" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6521" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4202" class="Function">count-is-emptyᵉ</a> <a id="6537" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6481" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="6539" class="Symbol">))</a>

          <a id="9179" href="foundation.propositional-truncations%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6110" class="Function">apply-universal-property-trunc-Propᵉ</a> <a id="9216" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8980" class="Bound">Lᵉ</a>

              <a id="9309" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16133" class="Function">is-equivalence-injective-Finᵉ</a> <a id="9339" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9340" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9353" class="Function">inv-equivᵉ</a> <a id="9351" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9273" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="9354" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14156" class="Function Operator">∘eᵉ</a> <a id="9358" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9147" class="Bound">eᵉ</a><a id="9360" class="Symbol">))))</a>

### If a type has cardinality `k` and cardinality `l`, then `k = l`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="eq-cardinalityᵉ"></a><a id="12426" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12426" class="Function">eq-cardinalityᵉ</a> <a id="12442" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="12446" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12447" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12447" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="12451" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12453" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="12458" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12460" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12461" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12461" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="12464" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12464" class="Bound">lᵉ</a> <a id="12467" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12469" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="12471" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12473" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12474" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12474" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="12477" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12479" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="12483" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12447" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a><a id="12486" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12488" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="12492" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3123" class="Function">has-cardinalityᵉ</a> <a id="12509" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12461" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="12512" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12474" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="12515" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12517" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3123" class="Function">has-cardinalityᵉ</a> <a id="12534" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12464" class="Bound">lᵉ</a> <a id="12537" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12474" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="12540" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12542" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2647" class="Datatype">Idᵉ</a> <a id="12546" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12461" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="12549" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12464" class="Bound">lᵉ</a>

### Equivalent finite types have the same cardinality

<pre class="Agda"><a id="eq-cardinality-equiv-is-finiteᵉ"></a><a id="12875" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12875" class="Function">eq-cardinality-equiv-is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="12907" class="Symbol">:</a>

### Any type of cardinality `k` is a set

### A finite type is contractible if and only if it has one element

    <a id="15726" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15728" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="15730" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15730" class="Bound">eᵉ</a> <a id="15733" class="Symbol">→</a>
      <a id="15741" href="foundation-core.contractible-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3162" class="Function">is-contr-equiv&#39;ᵉ</a>
        <a id="15766" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15768" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="15773" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#862" class="Function">1ᵉ</a><a id="15775" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="15785" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15787" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15789" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1298" class="Function">equiv-countᵉ</a> <a id="15802" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15730" class="Bound">eᵉ</a><a id="15804" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15806" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14156" class="Function Operator">∘eᵉ</a>
          <a id="15820" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15822" href="foundation.transport-along-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1592" class="Function">equiv-trᵉ</a> <a id="15832" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a>
            <a id="15849" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15851" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="15856" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15651" class="Bound">pᵉ</a> <a id="15859" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a> <a id="15862" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="15867" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15868" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11300" class="Function">compute-number-of-elements-is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="15906" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15730" class="Bound">eᵉ</a> <a id="15909" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15648" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="15911" class="Symbol">))))</a>
        <a id="15924" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15926" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5490" class="Function">is-contr-Fin-one-ℕᵉ</a><a id="15945" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="is-decidable-is-contr-is-finiteᵉ"></a><a id="15949" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15949" class="Function">is-decidable-is-contr-is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="15982" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="16105" href="foundation.decidable-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6739" class="Function">is-decidable-iffᵉ</a>
    <a id="16127" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16129" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15440" class="Function">is-contr-is-one-number-of-elements-is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="16175" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16098" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="16177" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>
### The type of all pairs consisting of a natural number `k` and a type of cardinality `k` is equivalent to the type of all finite types

<pre class="Agda"><a id="map-compute-total-UU-Finᵉ"></a><a id="16457" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16457" class="Function">map-compute-total-UU-Finᵉ</a> <a id="16483" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16485" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16486" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16486" class="Bound">lᵉ</a> <a id="16489" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16491" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="16496" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16498" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16500" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#585" class="Record">Σᵉ</a> <a id="16503" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16506" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16507" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3309" class="Function">UU-Finᵉ</a> <a id="16515" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16486" class="Bound">lᵉ</a><a id="16517" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16519" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16521" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2731" class="Function">𝔽ᵉ</a> <a id="16524" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16486" class="Bound">lᵉ</a>
<a id="16527" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#697" class="Field">pr1ᵉ</a> <a id="16532" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16533" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16457" class="Function">map-compute-total-UU-Finᵉ</a> <a id="16559" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16560" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="16566" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16566" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="16569" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16570" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="16576" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16576" class="Bound">Xᵉ</a> <a id="16579" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16579" class="Bound">eᵉ</a><a id="16581" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="16585" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16587" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16576" class="Bound">Xᵉ</a>
<a id="16590" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#711" class="Field">pr2ᵉ</a> <a id="16595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16596" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16457" class="Function">map-compute-total-UU-Finᵉ</a> <a id="16622" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16623" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="16629" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16629" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="16632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16633" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="16639" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16639" class="Bound">Xᵉ</a> <a id="16642" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16642" class="Bound">eᵉ</a><a id="16644" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="16648" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="16652" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9951" class="Function">is-finite-has-finite-cardinalityᵉ</a> <a id="16686" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16687" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#679" class="InductiveConstructor">pairᵉ</a> <a id="16693" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16629" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="16696" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16642" class="Bound">eᵉ</a><a id="16698" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="16794" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16796" href="foundation-core.functoriality-dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7790" class="Function">equiv-totᵉ</a>
    <a id="16811" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16813" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="16815" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16815" class="Bound">Xᵉ</a> <a id="16818" class="Symbol">→</a>
      <a id="16826" href="foundation.logical-equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5045" class="Function">equiv-iff-is-propᵉ</a>
        <a id="16853" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16855" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9377" class="Function">is-prop-has-finite-cardinalityᵉ</a><a id="16886" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="16896" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16898" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2391" class="Function">is-prop-is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="16917" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16815" class="Bound">Xᵉ</a><a id="16919" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="16929" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16931" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9951" class="Function">is-finite-has-finite-cardinalityᵉ</a><a id="16964" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="16974" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16976" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10631" class="Function">has-finite-cardinality-is-finiteᵉ</a><a id="17009" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="17013" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14156" class="Function Operator">∘eᵉ</a>
  <a id="17019" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17021" href="foundation.type-arithmetic-dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13356" class="Function">equiv-left-swap-Σᵉ</a><a id="17039" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Finite types are either inhabited or empty

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-inhabited-or-empty-is-finiteᵉ"></a><a id="17102" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17102" class="Function">is-inhabited-or-empty-is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="17135" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="17212" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17102" class="Function">is-inhabited-or-empty-is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="17245" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17246" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17246" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a><a id="17249" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17251" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17252" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17252" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a><a id="17254" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17256" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17256" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="17259" class="Symbol">=</a>

    <a id="17307" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17309" href="foundation.decidable-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9382" class="Function">is-inhabited-or-empty-Propᵉ</a> <a id="17337" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17252" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a><a id="17339" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="17345" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17347" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6099" class="Function">is-inhabited-or-empty-countᵉ</a><a id="17375" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Finite types of cardinality greater than one are inhabited

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-inhabited-type-UU-Fin-succ-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="17454" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17454" class="Function">is-inhabited-type-UU-Fin-succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17487" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="17491" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17492" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17492" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="17496" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17498" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="17503" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17505" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17506" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17506" class="Bound">nᵉ</a> <a id="17509" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17511" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="17513" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17515" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17516" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17516" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="17519" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17521" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3309" class="Function">UU-Finᵉ</a> <a id="17529" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17492" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="17533" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17534" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17542" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17506" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="17544" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="17547" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="17551" href="foundation.inhabited-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1224" class="Function">is-inhabitedᵉ</a> <a id="17565" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17566" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3406" class="Function">type-UU-Finᵉ</a> <a id="17579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17580" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17588" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17506" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="17590" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17592" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17516" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a><a id="17594" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="17596" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17454" class="Function">is-inhabited-type-UU-Fin-succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17629" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17629" class="Bound">nᵉ</a> <a id="17632" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17632" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="17635" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="17639" href="foundation.propositional-truncations%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6110" class="Function">apply-universal-property-trunc-Propᵉ</a>
    <a id="17680" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17682" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#711" class="Field">pr2ᵉ</a> <a id="17687" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17632" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a><a id="17689" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="17695" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17697" href="foundation.inhabited-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1130" class="Function">is-inhabited-Propᵉ</a> <a id="17716" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17717" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3406" class="Function">type-UU-Finᵉ</a> <a id="17730" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17731" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="17739" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17629" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="17741" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17743" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17632" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a><a id="17745" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="17752" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17754" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="17756" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17756" class="Bound">eᵉ</a> <a id="17759" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17761" href="foundation.propositional-truncations%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1593" class="Function">unit-trunc-Propᵉ</a> <a id="17778" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17779" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2892" class="Function">map-equivᵉ</a> <a id="17790" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17756" class="Bound">eᵉ</a> <a id="17793" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17794" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6036" class="Function">zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="17804" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17629" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="17806" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
### If `X` is finite, then its propositional truncation is decidable

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-decidable-type-trunc-Prop-is-finiteᵉ"></a><a id="17893" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17893" class="Function">is-decidable-type-trunc-Prop-is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="17933" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="17937" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17938" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17938" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="17942" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17944" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="17949" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17951" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17952" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17952" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="17955" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17957" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="17961" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17938" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a><a id="17964" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17966" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17968" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2285" class="Function">is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="17979" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17952" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="17982" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17984" href="foundation.decidable-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1541" class="Function">is-decidableᵉ</a> <a id="17998" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17999" href="foundation.propositional-truncations%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1500" class="Function">type-trunc-Propᵉ</a> <a id="18016" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17952" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a><a id="18018" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="18020" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17893" class="Function">is-decidable-type-trunc-Prop-is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="18060" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18060" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="18063" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="18067" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1998" class="Function">map-coproductᵉ</a>
    <a id="18086" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18088" href="foundation-core.function-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#309" class="Function">idᵉ</a><a id="18091" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="18097" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18099" href="foundation.propositional-truncations%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5725" class="Function">map-universal-property-trunc-Propᵉ</a> <a id="18134" href="foundation-core.empty-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2587" class="Function">empty-Propᵉ</a><a id="18145" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="18153" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18155" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17102" class="Function">is-inhabited-or-empty-is-finiteᵉ</a> <a id="18188" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18060" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="18190" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>

  <a id="is-finite-type-trunc-Propᵉ"></a><a id="18286" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18286" class="Function">is-finite-type-trunc-Propᵉ</a> <a id="18313" class="Symbol">:</a>

### We characterize the identity type of 𝔽

  <a id="19183" href="foundation-core.contractible-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3162" class="Function">is-contr-equiv&#39;ᵉ</a>

    <a id="19231" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19233" href="foundation-core.functoriality-dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7790" class="Function">equiv-totᵉ</a> <a id="19244" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19245" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18899" class="Function">extensionality-𝔽ᵉ</a> <a id="19263" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19176" class="Bound">Xᵉ</a><a id="19265" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="19272" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19274" href="foundation-core.torsorial-type-families%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2927" class="Function">is-torsorial-Idᵉ</a> <a id="19291" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19176" class="Bound">Xᵉ</a><a id="19293" class="Symbol">)</a>

### We characterize the identity type of `UU-Fin`
